I got in on a next day appointment - their system
Is very easy to use and book with. I ended up having to change times last minute and they were very accommodating.

My actual wax was with Bree. She was very sweet, asked questions about my previous wax experiences, and she was fast (which I like- it somehow hurts less).

I only took away a star because it was too fast - and when you‚Äôre that fast, you‚Äôre not very thorough. I felt a little rushed, and there were some areas she could‚Äôve taken more time on. But it‚Äôs an appointment based business so I get it- the more appointments you get the more money you get. I would definitely go back but I just know what to expect.

Heads up- they use a combination of hard wax and soft wax. Soft wax strips that top layer of skin causing some sensitivity. Just so you know.< /Review>

I was fully expecting to love this place after reading the reviews but my actual experience was lack luster. I scheduled a French bikini wax and face wax. After the waxer completed my face wax, I noticed that my sideburns were uneven and I had stray hairs left on my face. I immediately asked to use her tweezers to remove the stray hairs and I asked her to make my sideburns even. It took 2 attempts to even out my sideburns which left them shorter than desired. She kindly filled in my eyebrows after waxing them which I appreciated, but when I got home and removed the make up, I noticed stray hairs that I needed to clean up. I was mostly satisfied with my French bikini wax. My only complaint is that the top wasn't waxed in a straight line. My remaining hair is a bit slanted and oddly rounded at the top. I will say that the staff are friendly and professional. However, in my opinion, the outcome of the services and the experience did not align with the price point or my expectations. Unrelated to the service, the parking situation is a bit difficult to maneuver. Beware when entering the parking area or exiting, you may have to reverse to make room for a car coming toward you in the opposite direction.</review>

< Text>
Recently new to San Diego and I was on the hunt for a waxing studio. I am a travel nurse and have to find new waxing studios in every state I go to. With so many options I happened to come across this gem. This was the FIRST and ONLY place I tried. I booked my first visit with Angie for a Brazilian. I waited several days to see my results. I was so pleased that I went back in shortly after for my underarms. My appointment went smooth. I walked in, was greeted right away, offered a beverage, and waited only a few minutes until Angie came out. Angie is a really sweet and professional esthetician! Angie exceeded my expectations, she changed her gloves, never double dipped, and went from clean to dirty areas without cross contaminating. I am really glad I found this waxing studio. They offer an awesome monthly membership for Brazilians, which I highly recommend!</Text>

< Review>
I've been a loyal client every month since 2013 (it has gone thru a few name changes since then lol), and I would NEVER go anywhere else.  Hands down, this is the best wax boutique in the county.  I think I first found them (then 'Wax in the City') on Yelp - and was very impressed by the reviews, so decided to check it out.  The boutique is so cute.  The girls are the sweetest, most friendly people - and I love my Angie!  This place is Clean, clean, clean!   The wax they use is top of the line, and they use different types of wax on different parts - so they obviously know what they're doing.  And in all the years I have been going, I have Never seen anyone Double Dip!  Don't cancel last minute/no-show - it'll cost you!  These girls rely on their appointments, and they fill up quickly... I think walk-ins might have a tough time, because this place is regularly booked solid (but that's what happens when you're the best).  Their booking website is really easy to use, and you can make any changes to your appointment.  Hey!  If you're a student, you can get a special discount on Thursdays - I love that!  I have never been to their downtown location - but Angie only works at Normal Heights, so that's where I go.  I hear it's really nice, though.
Go. Ask for Angie. You won't be disappointed.< /Review>

< Text>
Great remnant of the original Polk Street gay bars!

The clientele does skew older, but I don't think I've ever come in here without having an interesting conversation with a number of people. Cute little outside patio that gets good sun in the afternoons, and the beer is cheap (even if the taps don't change very often).

< review>
Happy hour is a time when your friends are spending quality time with you, basically gossiping, while you stuff your faces with discounted food and drinks. One of my friends sent me a list of the top happy hour restaurants in the LA area from an article, so we can try new places together. This is one of those places, and it is soo worth it! This is in the Los Feliz area with their own parking lot! There is outdoor and indoor seating, and the place is pretty decent size so I doubt you would have to wait for a table or wait for too long.

Two problems with happy hour is the lack of selection, and the time. Most happy hours have a few cocktails, beer, and wine that's served with basically sliders and wings. Their list of happy hour foods is impressive. Yes, they do have the traditional sliders and wings, but also have turkey burger, Mac and cheese, soft pretzels, nachos, tacos, salad, chili hotdog, and churro with ice cream! Yes, they even have dessert on happy hour! Even their cocktail menu was pretty generous, and it did have wine and beer as well. The variety on the menu is very impressive, so there is something for everyone! The second issue with happy hour is the time because most end at 6pm. My friend doesn't even end her work until 6, and by the time we get there then it will be about 6:30. They end their happy hour at a decent time of 7pm! So that gave us enough time to order without feeling rushed.< /review>

<user>100343487869588737958<//user><Name>Gustavo Calderon<//Name><date>1558730806967</date><rate>1<//rate><text>This review is of the Blaze Franchise. Blaze Pizza is the new "Subway" of Pizza. Subway was very popular when it was new in the 80's until consumers realized its was made with cheap, unhealthy  ingredients and was not the sandwich they once thought. Blaze Pizza will follow that exact same path. It's a franchise that uses very low quality ingredients that require no skill to produce and the end result is a cheap pizza. They do not make pizza by hand but rather use a press machine for lack of skill or knowledge in the pizza making process. This is what franchises do. They teach inexperienced operators to produce cheap products while they collect a percentage of your gross sales. The dough does not have a proper fermentation time as they have limited space and time to produce a properly fermented dough ball. The result is a spongy dough that lacks crispness and good flavor.  The toppings do not taste or appear fresh  and would be considered the cheapest toppings that can put on a pizza. Understand that franchise made pizza will always be made with the cheapest ingredients using the least skilled process. Just think Pizza Hut, Domino's, Little Caesar's and soon to be Blaze Pizza. This franchise has no passion for producing a quality pizza but rather a desire to make a quick buck producing another lousy, franchise product.< /text>< pictures>

<text>If you need to get some work done or meet a friend for catch up -ILB is the spot.

The staff have never been crazy friendly here - and their menu (though sprinkled with healthy options) - has never been my favorite - but what Joe and the Juice does have going for it -is a plethora of chairs and tables, outlets to plug in your computer, easy wi-fi (without password), and a low key work environment.

Unlike most spots in the financial district - Joe & the Juice is open till 9 during the weekday - so you can easily grab a tea, juice, or little bite to eat - and just work to your heart's content.

I feel like I'm in New York City - typing away on a hightop table - seeing the bustle of downtown pass by the big windows beside me.

Trust.< /text>< userid>

She told me it would be 15-20 minutes. We left at 11:53 and returned at 12:30. The first girl appeared to walk back to the "workbench" where my watch was, fiddled with it a bit, then walked to me to explain the back needed to be put on. Then she asked the dark-haired, shorter, girl to assist. That girl finished my watch, came up to the counter, handed it to me. I noticed the inscription on the back was crooked and I made a comment.
